# Real-valued Cases
ieee_test_50000 = {
    set_temp_variable = { arg_a = 2136.175 }
    set_temp_variable = { arg_b = 2136.175 }

    ieeeMul = yes
    set_temp_variable = { actual_output = out_a }

    set_temp_variable = { expected_output = 0.000 }

    if = {
        limit = {
            NOT = { check_variable = { actual_output = expected_output } }
        }
        log = "Test [?test_id] - +VAL00  * +VAL00  - FAIL"
        add_to_temp_array = { test_fail_array = test_id }
    }
    else = {
        log = "Test [?test_id] - +VAL00  * +VAL00  - PASS"
    }

    set_temp_variable = { to_print_float = actual_output }
    log = "Actual: [print_float_full]"
    set_temp_variable = { to_print_float = expected_output }
    log = "Expect: [print_float_full]"
}

    set_temp_variable = { arg_b = 2139095.040 }

    ieeeMul = yes
    set_temp_variable = { actual_output = out_a }

    set_temp_variable = { expected_output = -8388.608 }

    if = {
        limit = {
            NOT = { check_variable = { actual_output = expected_output } }
        }
        log = "Test [?test_id] - -VAL09  * +INFNTY - FAIL"
        add_to_temp_array = { test_fail_array = test_id }
    }
    else = {
        log = "Test [?test_id] - -VAL09  * +INFNTY - PASS"
    }

    set_temp_variable = { to_print_float = actual_output }
    log = "Actual: [print_float_full]"
    set_temp_variable = { to_print_float = expected_output }
    log = "Expect: [print_float_full]"
}

    set_temp_variable = { arg_b = -2147483.648 }

    ieeeMul = yes
    set_temp_variable = { actual_output = out_a }

    set_temp_variable = { expected_output = 2143289.344 }

    if = {
        limit = {
            NOT = {
                OR = {
                    check_variable = { actual_output > 2139095.040 }
                    AND = {
                        check_variable = { actual_output > -8388.608 }
                        check_variable = { actual_output < 0 }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        log = "Test [?test_id] - -INFNTY * -ZERO   - FAIL"
        add_to_temp_array = { test_fail_array = test_id }
    }
    else = {
        log = "Test [?test_id] - -INFNTY * -ZERO   - PASS"
    }

    set_temp_variable = { to_print_float = actual_output }
    log = "Actual: [print_float_full]"
    set_temp_variable = { to_print_float = expected_output }
    log = "Expect: [print_float_full]"
}

# NaN Cases
ieee_test_50900 = {
    set_temp_variable = { arg_a = 2136.175 }
    set_temp_variable = { arg_b = 2143289.344 }

    ieeeMul = yes
    set_temp_variable = { actual_output = out_a }

    set_temp_variable = { expected_output = 2143289.344 }

    if = {
        limit = {
            NOT = {
                OR = {
                    check_variable = { actual_output > 2139095.040 }
                    AND = {
                        check_variable = { actual_output > -8388.608 }
                        check_variable = { actual_output < 0 }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        log = "Test [?test_id] - +VAL00  * +POSNAN - FAIL"
        add_to_temp_array = { test_fail_array = test_id }
    }
    else = {
        log = "Test [?test_id] - +VAL00  * +POSNAN - PASS"
    }

    set_temp_variable = { to_print_float = actual_output }
    log = "Actual: [print_float_full]"
    set_temp_variable = { to_print_float = expected_output }
    log = "Expect: [print_float_full]"
}
ieee_test_50901 = {
    set_temp_variable = { arg_a = 2143289.344 }
    set_temp_variable = { arg_b = 2136.175 }

    ieeeMul = yes
    set_temp_variable = { actual_output = out_a }

    set_temp_variable = { expected_output = 2143289.344 }

    if = {
        limit = {
            NOT = {
                OR = {
